## ⚡ SESSION PROTOCOL — READ THIS FIRST

> **Storage strategy:** CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md lives **locally** in the `PRVS RO Dashboard` Cowork workspace folder (primary). GitHub is a **backup only**, pushed at end of session. Always read from local. Always write to local first.

### 🟢 START OF SESSION — Roland's command:
> *"Read CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md from the workspace folder before doing anything else. Confirm the workspace is on `pre-prod` (default working branch) — if not, switch via `git checkout pre-prod`. Run the drift check: `git log main..pre-prod --oneline` AND `git log pre-prod..main --oneline`. The hard invariant is that `pre-prod..main` MUST be empty (`main` is never ahead of `pre-prod`); if it returns anything, that is Session-83-class drift — surface it and resolve via fast-forward back-merge before any other work. `main..pre-prod` returning commits is fine (unreleased work soaking on pre-prod). Confirm the current index.html version matches the File Inventory. Read the Active TODO List out loud to me grouped by priority. Flag any 🔴 blocking issues or Roland-action items still pending. Follow the Start of Session Checklist in that file. Then ask: 'Is there anything else to add or change before we start?' and wait for my answer before beginning any work."*

If it returns ANYTHING, that is the Session-83-class drift (`main` ahead of `pre-prod`) — surface it and resolve via a fast-forward back-merge (`git checkout pre-prod && git merge main && git push origin pre-prod`) before any other work. `git log main..pre-prod` returning commits is OK — that is just unreleased work soaking on `pre-prod`; note what's pending promotion but do not treat it as an error (see 🌿 BRANCH MODEL → Drift Prevention Rules and the 🔒 END-SESSION BRANCH SYNC GATE).

### 🔒 END-SESSION BRANCH SYNC GATE

> **Added 2026-05-31 (Session 84) after the Session 83 doc-drift.** Session 83 shipped v1.429 + v1.430 to `main` correctly (production was never at risk), but the End-Session doc commit (`13c80b5`, `CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md` + `CLAUDE_CONTEXT_HISTORY.md` only) landed on `main` **without** syncing `pre-prod`, and the "pre-prod ≡ main verified" claim was reported from memory instead of actually run. Result: `main` sat one doc commit AHEAD of `pre-prod` until Session 84 Start caught it. This gate makes the sync a real, pasted-output assertion that cannot be faked.

> 🚨 **ROOT CAUSE — this gate OVERRIDES the `prvs-end-session` skill's STEP 4.** The live skill hardcodes `git add … && git commit && git push origin main` with **no `pre-prod` awareness** — it predates the pre-prod branch model (codified Session 79). That bare `git push origin main` is the literal mechanism that caused the Session 83 drift. **Ignore the skill's STEP 4 push command and run THIS gate instead.** The skill source must be patched in the plugin to match (Session 84 TODO); until it is, this CLAUDE_CONTEXT gate is the binding authority — the skill's own STEP 2 already instructs Claude to follow the CLAUDE_CONTEXT checklist, so this override is in force every session.

**The mandatory invariant (memorize this):** `git log pre-prod..main --oneline` MUST be empty — **`main` must never contain a commit that `pre-prod` lacks.** That is the exact condition Session 83 violated. The reverse, `git log main..pre-prod --oneline`, MAY legitimately show commits — that is just unreleased work soaking on `pre-prod` awaiting promotion, which is normal and fine.

**Core rule:** the End-Session doc commit is ALWAYS made on `pre-prod` first, then promoted forward to `main` ONLY if a release shipped this session. Forward-only flow (pre-prod → main) is preserved; `main` only ever moves by fast-forward from `pre-prod`.

**Run the matching case. Paste the REAL output of every `rev-parse` — never declare the session complete from memory.**

**CASE A — NO release shipped this session** (work stayed on pre-prod; main untouched):
```
git checkout pre-prod
git add -A && git commit -m "Session NN End — <summary>"
git push origin pre-prod
# HARD ASSERTION — these two MUST print identical hashes:
git rev-parse pre-prod
git rev-parse origin/pre-prod
# INVARIANT CHECK — this MUST print nothing (main is not ahead of pre-prod):
git log pre-prod..main --oneline
```
`main` legitimately stays behind by the doc commit (and any other unreleased pre-prod work) until the next release promotes pre-prod → main. Next Start Session's drift check will show `main..pre-prod` non-empty (expected) and `pre-prod..main` empty (required). Record the pending-promotion delta in the Session Log.

**CASE B — a release SHIPPED to main this session:**
```
# 1. Commit the doc update on pre-prod (NEVER directly on main):
git checkout pre-prod
git add -A && git commit -m "Session NN End — <summary>"
git push origin pre-prod
# 2. Promote forward to main (fast-forward only):
git checkout main
git pull --ff-only origin main
git merge --ff-only pre-prod
git push origin main
# 3. Tag the release:
git tag v1.XXX && git push origin v1.XXX
# 4. HARD ASSERTION — all FOUR MUST print the SAME hash:
git rev-parse main
git rev-parse origin/main
git rev-parse pre-prod
git rev-parse origin/pre-prod
# 5. Leave workspace on the default working branch:
git checkout pre-prod
```
If any of the four hashes differs in Case B, the session is **NOT complete** — resolve before declaring done.

**Why this prevents a repeat:** the old steps let the doc commit land on whichever branch happened to be checked out (it was `main` in Session 83) and treated the sync verification as a checkbox rather than a gate. Pinning the doc commit to `pre-prod` + forward-only promotion + a pasted hash assertion removes both the ambiguity and the ability to report success without proof.

## 🛑 SESSION WORKFLOW RULES

These rules govern HOW Claude collaborates with Roland during the session, separate from non-negotiable code rules.

### Rule: One step at a time — never bundle commands with forward-looking questions

When Claude asks Roland to run a command, test, or query (DevTools console, SQL, CLI — anything that needs Roland's action):

1. **Explain HOW to run it BEFORE listing the command.** Examples:
   - DevTools console queries: *"paste ONE LINE AT A TIME and hit Enter; the console only echoes the LAST expression, so a block-paste of multiple queries only returns the last one's value."*
   - Supabase SQL: *"paste the full block into Supabase SQL Editor and Run."*
   - Don't assume Roland knows the console / shell / IDE quirks for the tool in question.
2. **WAIT** for Roland to run it and paste back the result.
3. **Verify** the result against expected return values.
4. **Only after verification passes**, ask about the next step (next phase, branch strategy, deploy / merge, scope question, etc.).

**Never bundle "run X" + "tell me Y" in the same response.** If Roland is being asked to validate something AND choose a future direction in the same turn, he can't answer the direction question without first running the validation — and if the validation fails, his direction answer is moot. Phase-verification steps must be STOP-AND-VALIDATE gates, not stack-and-continue.

**Added 2026-05-25 (Session 75)** after Roland called this out during Phase 1 modularization verification:
> *"We can't move forward with commands until I validate the command return. Stop giving me commands to run simultaneously to giving me tests to run with verified or questionable responses."*

Persisted to both CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md AND Claude's auto-memory ([[one-step-at-a-time]]) so the rule survives a memory wipe.

## 🌿 BRANCH MODEL

> Established 2026-05-26 (Session 79) after the Phase 4.5 merge proved the topic-branch-then-FF-merge pattern. All work follows this model going forward — no exceptions without Roland's explicit approval in chat.

### Branch Tiers

| Branch | Role | Receives From | Promotes To |
|---|---|---|---|
| `main` | **Production** — auto-deploys to GitHub Pages within ~60s of push | fast-forward merges from `pre-prod`; emergency merges from `hotfix/*` | (terminal — nothing) |
| `pre-prod` | **Default working / integration branch** — Roland tests locally here before promoting to main | direct commits (low-risk work); fast-forward merges from `refactor/*` and `feature/*` topic branches; back-merges from `main` after hotfixes | fast-forward merge to `main` when stable |
| `refactor/<topic>` or `feature/<topic>` | **Isolated high-risk work** — auth, RLS, schema migrations, big multi-file refactors, anything with rollback risk | direct commits | fast-forward merge to `pre-prod` |
| `hotfix/<topic>` | **Emergency production patch** — used ONLY when production is broken (security, broken auth, data loss) | direct commits | fast-forward merge to `main` AND back-merge to `pre-prod` (mandatory same-session) |

### Workflow Patterns

**Normal session** (low/medium risk work):
1. Claude checks out `pre-prod` at session start.
2. Drift check: `git log main..pre-prod --oneline` AND `git log pre-prod..main --oneline`. Hard invariant: `pre-prod..main` MUST be empty (`main` never ahead of `pre-prod`). `main..pre-prod` may show unreleased work soaking on pre-prod — that's fine. If `pre-prod..main` returns anything, surface and resolve (fast-forward back-merge) before any work.
3. Work happens on `pre-prod` directly. Claude edits, Roland commits + pushes (per the `feedback_claude_edits_roland_git` memory rule).
4. Roland tests locally against `pre-prod` via `python3 -m http.server 8765` from a pre-prod checkout.
5. When stable, Roland fast-forwards main: `git checkout main && git pull --ff-only origin main && git merge --ff-only pre-prod && git push origin main`.
6. If a version bumped, tag the release on main: `git tag v1.XXX && git push origin v1.XXX`.
7. Live-URL verify on production GitHub Pages.

**High-risk session** (auth, RLS, schema, big refactor):
1. Branch off pre-prod: `git checkout pre-prod && git checkout -b refactor/<topic>` (or `feature/<topic>`).
2. Work + commit on the topic branch.
3. Local verification matrix on the topic branch (per session-specific test plan).
4. Fast-forward merge into pre-prod: `git checkout pre-prod && git pull --ff-only origin pre-prod && git merge --ff-only refactor/<topic> && git push origin pre-prod`.
5. Soak period on pre-prod (length varies by risk — sometimes overnight, sometimes a few hours).
6. Fast-forward merge pre-prod → main when ready (Normal session step 5).
7. Delete the topic branch local + remote: `git branch -d refactor/<topic> && git push origin --delete refactor/<topic>`.

**Hotfix flow** (emergency only — production is broken):
1. Branch off main directly: `git checkout main && git pull --ff-only origin main && git checkout -b hotfix/<topic>`.
2. Commit message prefix: `HOTFIX:` (e.g., `HOTFIX: revert auth.js loadUserRoles change causing silent demote`). Makes hotfixes trivially greppable in `git log`.
3. Tag the fix commit: `git tag hotfix-YYYY-MM-DD-<slug> && git push origin hotfix-YYYY-MM-DD-<slug>`.
4. Fast-forward merge into main: `git checkout main && git merge --ff-only hotfix/<topic> && git push origin main`.
5. **MANDATORY same-session back-merge** to keep pre-prod in sync: `git checkout pre-prod && git merge main && git push origin pre-prod`. No "I'll do it later." No exceptions. This is THE rule that prevents drift.
6. Add an entry to the 🚨 HOTFIX LOG section (below the Key Architecture Decisions section) — date, what broke, what fixed it, commit hashes, back-merge commit hash.
7. Delete the hotfix branch local + remote.

### Drift Prevention Rules

1. **Mandatory back-merge after hotfix.** Any `hotfix/*` → `main` push MUST be immediately followed by `git checkout pre-prod && git merge main && git push origin pre-prod`, in the same session. No exceptions. This is THE most important drift rule.
2. **Drift check at session start.** START SESSION runs `git log main..pre-prod --oneline` AND `git log pre-prod..main --oneline`. **Hard invariant: `pre-prod..main` MUST be empty — `main` must never contain a commit `pre-prod` lacks (this is the exact condition Session 83 violated via a doc commit pushed to main only).** `main..pre-prod` returning commits is allowed (unreleased work soaking on pre-prod). If `pre-prod..main` is non-empty, flag and resolve via fast-forward back-merge before any other work. The End-Session doc commit is pinned to `pre-prod` first precisely to keep this invariant true — see 🔒 END-SESSION BRANCH SYNC GATE.
3. **Hotfix log.** Every hotfix gets a row in the 🚨 HOTFIX LOG section below. Date, trigger, fix, main commit, back-merge commit, branches synced.
4. **Hotfix commit message convention.** Prefix `HOTFIX:` in every hotfix commit. Tag the fix commit `hotfix-YYYY-MM-DD-<slug>`.
5. **Tag every release.** When pre-prod merges to main with a version bump, tag main with the new version (`git tag v1.XXX && git push origin v1.XXX`). Makes rollback trivial; gives GitHub Releases a target.
6. **Delete merged branches.** Post-merge, delete the topic branch local + remote (`git branch -d <name> && git push origin --delete <name>`). Keeps `git branch -a` clean and prevents confusion about active vs stale work.
7. **Cap feature branch life at 7 days.** If a `refactor/*` or `feature/*` branch goes past a week, weekly-merge `pre-prod` INTO the branch (`git merge pre-prod` on the branch) to keep it from diverging. The longer a branch lives, the harder the eventual merge.
8. **Forward-only flow.** Code flows feature → pre-prod → main (forward). Hotfixes flow hotfix → main → pre-prod (back-merge). Any other merge direction needs an explicit reason in the commit message.

### When in Doubt

A topic branch is cheaper than a regression. If a change feels risky or touches auth/RLS/schema/multi-file/multi-table — branch first, ask Roland later. The 30-second cost of `git checkout -b refactor/foo` has saved hours of revert work many times in this project's history.

| 🟡 | — | **POST-MODULARIZATION: Fix Cowork sandbox FUSE lock-file pattern once and for all** | **Recurring blocker across Sessions 64, 65, 67, 69, 70, 71, 72, 73, 75 (every session that does meaningful git work).** Cowork mounts `~/rv-dashboard` into the sandbox via a FUSE shim. The shim grants reads + file creation fine, but `unlink()` on `.git/index.lock`, `.git/HEAD.lock`, `.git/refs/heads/<branch>.lock`, and `.git/objects/<xx>/tmp_obj_*` returns `EPERM` — so git's standard create-then-unlink pattern leaves stale locks behind. Every commit/push from the sandbox requires Roland to subsequently `find ~/rv-dashboard/.git -name '*.lock' -print -delete` from the Mac terminal. Has caused: (a) staged-but-not-pushed code that looks like a bug; (b) "branch is behind" + "modifications would be overwritten" errors on pull even when working tree IS the latest; (c) wasted minutes per session clearing locks. **Workarounds in use:** git plumbing via `commit-tree` + direct-SHA-to-origin push, deferring local ref updates. **Real fix:** Cowork sandbox layer (Anthropic side) should permit `unlink()` on `.git/*.lock` and `.git/objects/<xx>/tmp_obj_*` patterns. Alternatives if Anthropic can't fix: (a) auto-clear-locks bash wrapper around every git op; (b) move all git ops to Mac terminal and use sandbox only for file edits; (c) provide a non-FUSE workspace path for `.git/` specifically. **Deferred until modularization is complete** per Roland 2026-05-25 Session 75 — do NOT chase this squirrel mid-refactor. Track as a Cowork product-feedback item too. | ⏳ Open (post-refactor) |
| 🟡 | GH#33 Phase 2 | **Systemic historical dupe scan across all time_logs** | After Phase 1 has a week of real-world data to collect a baseline rejection-rate, run a full-table scan to find all (tech, ro) pairs with 2+ clock-ins within 30s. Use CTE: `GROUP BY tech_email, ro_id, DATE_TRUNC('minute', clock_in) HAVING count(*) > 1 AND max(clock_in)-min(clock_in) < interval '30 seconds'`. Preview → Roland reviews → batch delete per rule (prefer rows with real tech-initiated clock_out over synthetic `auto_eod_*`). Session 53 manually cleaned Scott Kline's RO only (7 rows). Other ROs likely have similar dupes lurking. ~2h session. | ⏳ Open — after 1 week of Phase 1 baseline |

Debounce: require 5 seconds between successful clock-ins on same tech across all ROs (catches confused tech tapping between adjacent RO buttons). Metric view: log-based alert if 23505 count >5 per day (signals upstream client bug). ~30min. | ⏳ Optional |
| 🟡 | GH#34 | **Offline-queue clock_out race with auto-logout (edge case)** | **Observed theoretically Session 52.** If a tech is offline for >12 hours straight (rare but possible with no cell signal), queues a clock_out in IndexedDB at 6 PM, then the cron runs at 9 PM and auto-closes the session at `clock_in + 12h` — when the phone later reconnects and replays the queued clock_out, it `UPDATE`s an already-closed row and overwrites `close_reason='auto_eod'` with the real 6 PM timestamp (but clears the auto_eod marker). Not wrong per se, but the audit trail is misleading. Fix: conditional write in the offline-queue replay — `UPDATE ... WHERE clock_out IS NULL` so the replay no-ops if already closed. Low priority until it becomes a real issue. | ⏳ Open |
| 🟠 | GH#36 | **Realtime sync + auto-refresh — fix stale dashboard symptoms** | **Session 56 (2026-04-25).** Investigation of "status reverts to Not On Lot" complaint (GH#29c) showed every status change is correctly attributed to a real user — there is NO code-level revert. Root cause is **multi-user race + stale-tab data**: staff A changes status, staff B's open tab still shows the old value, staff B "corrects" it based on stale data, looks like a revert. Same root cause behind two other annoying symptoms Roland flagged: (1) tech/manager creates an RO and saves it, but other staff's dashboards don't show it without a hard refresh; (2) dashboards left open for hours show outdated data until manually reloaded. **Two-phase fix.** **Phase 1 — Periodic auto-reload (cheap, ~30 min).** Add `setInterval(loadDataFromSupabase, 90_000)` (or similar window) to `index.html` after initial load. Reuses existing data-loading code. Tabs left open auto-refresh every 90 sec. Trade-off: short staleness window remains, mild network cost. Same pattern can be added to `worklist-report.html`, `closed-ros.html`, `analytics.html` independently. Ship first as immediate relief. **Phase 2 — Supabase Realtime subscription (~1 session).** Subscribe to `repair_orders` Postgres changes via `supabase.channel()` → on INSERT, push the new row into `currentData` and re-render; on UPDATE, patch the matching row by `_supabaseId` (uses the v1.408 UUID-first lookup pattern); on DELETE / soft-delete, drop the row. Show a small "Brandon just changed Mauricio's RO to On Lot" toast for cross-user changes (visible to admins/sr_managers only — silent for the user who made the change). Also subscribe `notes`, `parts`, `manager_work_lists` for fuller coverage. Phase 2 supersedes Phase 1's setInterval (remove it once realtime is solid). **Closes the GH#29c monitor entry as expected — multi-user UX problem, not a code bug.** | ⏳ Open — Phase 1 first |

All state reads via `window.X`; all state writes via explicit `window.X = Y` (strict-mode modules throw on undeclared assignments). Defensive `typeof window.X === 'function'` guards on cross-module call sites (loadDataFromSupabase, renderBoard, updateViewModeDropdown, loadStaff, loadAppConfig, etc.) so the module can boot in any test order. Window bridge at bottom attaches all 19 exports — overwrites inline auto-globalized versions with behaviorally-identical module versions. DevTools-verified equivalence both phases. Inline copies in index.html UNTOUCHED runtime-wise; 6 PHASE 4B-C + 3 PHASE 4B-D MIGRATED comment blocks added above them. **Phase 4.5 (delete inline copies) unlocked** — next session's headline task. |

| `time-off.html` | **v1.3** | GH#38 Phase 1 — Employee Time Off page. All-role access (Google SSO + Supabase, storageKey `prvs_timeoff_auth`). Self-service sick/vacation/personal/general time off requests with backdating. Calendar view (monthly grid, colored first-name chips per type), List view (table + delete), Stats strip (days by type + total for selected year/employee filter). No approval workflow — records logged directly. Linked from 🏖 Time Off header button on index.html (all authenticated users). DB: `time_off_requests` table with generated `total_days` column + `partial_hours NUMERIC(4,1)`, RLS, updated_at trigger. **Notification system (Session 57, commit 2d65f95):** `fireTimeOffNotifications()` fires on every submit — (1) immediate `send-quote-email` `time_off_notify` call with `context='submitted'` to all active sr_manager/manager/admin staff; (2) `scheduled_notifications` day-before row (8 AM CDT = 13:00 UTC on day before startDate); (3) `scheduled_notifications` morning-of row (8 AM CDT on startDate). Day-before + morning-of only inserted when `startDate > today` (no ghost rows for backdated entries). Fire-and-forget — never blocks the UI. **v1.1 (Session 62, 2026-04-30, commit 8ec431d):** Employee dropdown removed from request modal — all users submit for themselves only. Manager view-side filter bar preserved. `loadStaff()` modal population block removed; `isManagerOrAbove()` branch in `submitRequest()` removed; stale `modalEmployee` DOM reference cleaned up. **v1.2 (Session 62, 2026-04-30, commit 8ec431d):** Full Day / Partial Day toggle. `partial_hours NUMERIC(4,1)` nullable column on DB (NULL = full day, 0.5–8.0 = partial hours). `dayValue(r)` helper: `partial_hours/8` for partial, else `total_days`. `fmtStat(n)` helper: clean decimal display (strips trailing zeros). Stats strip uses both helpers for fractional accuracy. Calendar chips: `⏱ FirstName Xh` for partials. List view: blue `⏱ Xh` chip + "same day" end date for partials. Reason field required for ALL requests (notes column, renamed in UI). `loadTimeOffData()` SELECT includes `partial_hours` (omitting it would leave all partial display logic broken). `fireTimeOffNotifications()` accepts `partialHours` param, computes `durationLabel`. Migration: `add_partial_hours_to_time_off.sql` (Roland ran 2026-04-30). **v1.3 (Session 68, 2026-05-18, commit `cfab831`):** Admin-only employee picker restored on request modal. New `#modalEmployeeGroup` div (hidden by default) sits at top of modal-body. `loadStaff()` populates it with all active staff when `isAdmin()` returns true; admin themselves labeled `(you)`. `openRequestModal()` pre-selects the admin on every open (default = submit for self). `submitRequest()` admin branch: reads selected employee, writes `employee_email` + `employee_name` for that person, keeps `submitted_by_email` = logged-in admin (preserves audit trail in List view's *Submitted By* column). Notification email automatically reflects the selected employee (no code change needed — `fireTimeOffNotifications` already takes empEmail/empName by value). Non-admin roles (Sr Manager / Manager / Tech) unchanged — self-submit only. No DB migration required (schema already supported this attribution pattern from v1.0). |

CHECK constraint on `repair_orders.status` AND `cashiered.status` enforcing the 11-status canonical set: 'Not On Lot', 'On Lot', 'Scheduled', 'Awaiting Approval', 'Awaiting parts', 'Ready to Work', 'In progress', 'Repairs Completed', 'Waiting for QA/QC', 'Ready for pickup', 'Delivered/Cashed Out'. Sets `repair_orders.status` column default to 'Not On Lot' (closes L-2 from Session 72 scan re: solar.html `createRO` NULL-status inserts). Both constraints `is_validated=true` post-apply. Bug class now mechanically impossible at the DB layer regardless of which HTML file writes the status. Rollback SQL included in file. |

Executive summary + 1 BLOCKING (B-1 closed-ros.html — already patched in this session) + 1 BLOCKING (B-2 backfill blind-spot explanation: Session 71 backfill's `AND deleted_at IS NULL` clause is why 3 capital-P rows survived; harmless because they're tombstoned) + 2 HIGH (H-1 no DB CHECK constraint — fixed this session via `status_casing_check_constraint.sql`; H-2 `ALL_STATUSES` array in index.html missing 'Scheduled' — open) + 3 MEDIUM (M-1 no shared constants module across HTML files; M-2 defensive Spanish duplicate-casing keys in i18n map; M-3 cross-table casing inconsistency) + 3 LOW (L-1 display-vs-value asymmetry; L-2 solar.html `createRO` omits status — closed this session via column default; L-3 minor). Recommended fix order + full DB migration SQL + literal census appendix. Carried-forward items go to backlog. |
| `supabase/migrations/cron_archive_cashiered_ros.sql` | — | **Session 61 (2026-04-29):** Creates `archive_cashiered_ros()` SECURITY DEFINER function + pg_cron job `archive-cashiered-ros` scheduled every Saturday 22:00 UTC (= 5 PM CDT). Function loops `repair_orders WHERE status='Delivered/Cashed Out' AND deleted_at IS NULL`, inserts into `cashiered` (full field mapping), then hard-deletes from `repair_orders`. `ON CONFLICT (original_ro_id) DO NOTHING` — idempotent. Days-on-lot prefers `date_arrived` over `date_received`. Week label matches `getWeekLabel()` JS logic. GRANT EXECUTE to postgres + service_role. Commit `1b54a319`. **Roland must run in Supabase SQL Editor to activate the Saturday archiver.** |

## ⚠️ Known Issues & Gotchas

### NEVER hand Roland an unguarded ER status-change SQL — a bare multi-statement close-out mass-corrupted enhancement_requests (Session 125 incident, 2026-06-26)
A two-statement ER close-out (`UPDATE enhancement_requests SET status='done', completion_notes=..., test_steps=... WHERE id='X' AND status <> 'done';` x2, pasted into the Supabase SQL editor) executed with NO effective WHERE on the second statement — it set status='done' + the WO-reorder completion_notes on **ALL 59 rows**. That fired `trg_notify_er_completion` for every transition into `done`, sending **~13 wrong "your request is live" emails** to requesters (12:56 UTC), and **overwrote the completion_notes** of ~23 historically-completed ERs. The editor reported "Success" with no error. Root cause: on a copy-pasted multi-statement UPDATE the `WHERE` was dropped/mangled and silently became a full-table write. **Recovery that worked (all run by Roland, verified read-only by me):** identify corrupted rows by the WO-note signature (`completion_notes LIKE 'In the Build/Edit Work Order form%'`) + the 12:56 `completion_emailed_at` stamps; revert wrongly-flipped rows to their pre-state (unreviewed/in-progress/declined) in small `id IN (...)` UPDATEs **each carrying a redundant blast-radius guard** (`completion_emailed_at >= '...12:50'` and/or the WO-note LIKE) so a dropped predicate can't nuke the table; reconstruct lost completion_notes from the INTACT `description` (admin_notes were only appended-to, never overwritten — so each ER's original request text survived) + version history; add `RETURNING id` to every write so the editor shows exactly which rows changed. **RULES going forward:** (1) every data-changing SQL handed over = a SINGLE guarded statement with an explicit `id IN (...)` PLUS a second redundant guard column; (2) always append `RETURNING id` and check the returned count before trusting it; (3) never trust "Success. No rows returned." (4) Remember flipping an ER into `done` emails the requester, so a mass mis-flip = mass mis-email. Recovery notes: PITR is an UNenabled Supabase add-on here; daily scheduled backups exist (e.g. 04:14 UTC) but "Restore" is whole-DB in-place (would lose the workday's live data); "Restore to new project (BETA)" can clone to a throwaway project for an exact table-level copy-back, but we declined it for low-value historical notes on closed ERs. (Memory: [[feedback_guard_er_status_sql]].)

### NEVER schedule an autonomous sandbox-git PROD promotion for PRVS (Session 124 incident, 2026-06-25)
A scheduled one-time task set to FF pre-prod -> main + tag + regression FIRED at its trigger time and ran git **in the sandbox** against the Mac repo's `.git` (the sandbox mounts it via FUSE). It collided with stale `.lock` files it could not remove ("Operation not permitted"), half-completed the fast-forward, and left: HEAD parked on `main`, a dirty working tree (pre-prod content sitting on old main), and a `v1.461` tag created AND pushed onto the WRONG commit (old prod `e69b4f6` instead of the release `e927270`). **Production was not corrupted** (origin/main stayed at the last-good commit) but the promotion did not complete. Two compounding causes: (a) sandbox git against the FUSE-shared repo cannot manage lock files and clashes with the Mac's git; (b) the task was disabled at 5:38 for a 5:15 fireAt — disabling AFTER the trigger time does nothing. **Recovery that worked:** on the Mac, `rm -f .git/*.lock .git/refs/**/*.lock`; confirm `git diff origin/pre-prod` is empty (nothing lost); `git reset --hard origin/pre-prod` while on main (a clean FF since old main is an ancestor); `git push origin main`; `git tag -d v1.461 && git push origin :refs/tags/v1.461`; recreate `git tag v1.461 <correct-sha> && git push origin v1.461`; verify the four-hash Sync Gate. **RULE:** PRVS prod promotions are INTERACTIVE (Roland runs git on the Mac, Claude does the Chrome regression). A scheduled task may only NOTIFY/remind — never execute git itself. If one is ever scheduled, cancel it well BEFORE its trigger time. (Memory: [[feedback_no_scheduled_sandbox_git_prvs]].)

### Supabase is removing default public-schema Data API grants — new tables after 2026-10-30 need explicit GRANT (Session 124, 2026-06-25)
Supabase email (2026-06-25): new `public` tables will no longer be auto-exposed to the Data API (PostgREST/GraphQL/supabase-js via anon + authenticated). New projects: 2026-05-30. Existing projects (PRVS, ref axfejhudchdejoiwaetq): enforced on NEW tables 2026-10-30. **Existing PRVS tables are unaffected.** The risk: the project's table-creation migrations set up RLS policies ONLY and rely on the default auto-grant (e.g. `woosender_leads.sql` has `enable row level security` + `create policy` but NO `grant`). A table created with that pattern AFTER 2026-10-30 will return permission-denied despite correct RLS. **FIX (adopt now, harmless before the deadline):** add `grant select, insert, update, delete on public.<table> to authenticated;` (+ `grant select ... to anon;` only if a page reads with the anon key) to every new-table migration. `service_role` (edge fns) is unaffected. Next table-creating work (messaging-automation P1 notification_queue/message_templates) should include the grants. (Memory: [[reference_supabase_public_grant_change]].)

### WooSender lead intake is LIVE — capture edge fn + admin review queue (Session 123, 2026-06-24)
WooSender Won-stage leads flow in via the dev's Zapier outbound webhook (Webhooks-by-Zapier POST, **custom header, NOT Basic Auth**) -> the `woosender-intake` edge fn -> the `woosender_leads` review-queue table -> the admin-only `leads.html` page. Key facts for next session: (1) the webhook auth is a SHARED SECRET — header `x-prvs-webhook-secret` must equal the `WOOSENDER_WEBHOOK_SECRET` edge-fn secret (set via `supabase secrets set`); a missing/wrong secret returns 401 with no DB row. (2) The WooSender JSON envelope is **identical across pipelines** — the same keys every time; lean lead forms just send empty strings (extraction maps "" -> null). The service/silo is derived from `opportunity.pipeline` (roof->Roof, solar->Solar), NOT the often-empty `clientServiceNeeds`. (3) `woosender_id` = `contactGuid` (stable per-lead key, present even on lean forms) is used for re-fire idempotency. (4) `review_status` CHECK = new/promoted/merged/dismissed/duplicate (the `merged` value was added by a follow-up ALTER; constraint `woosender_leads_review_status_check`). (5) `leads.html` is **admin-only** (`isAdmin()` gate) and reaches the live DB — Promote creates a REAL RO and Merge updates a REAL RO + adds a `customer_comm` note (the call transcript lands in the RO's 💬 Customer Comm section). (6) The phone dedupe matches digits-only (repair_orders phones are stored in mixed formats like `(916) 240-1344`). To extend the mapping when new pipelines appear, look at `raw_payload` first — do not assume field names. (7) **RLS needs BOTH a SELECT and an UPDATE policy** — the original migration shipped SELECT-only, so Promote/Merge/Dismiss (authenticated UPDATEs from leads.html) silently matched 0 rows with NO error and the lead never left the queue (RO updated fine because repair_orders has its own update policy). Fixed S123 by adding `"Authenticated can update woosender_leads"` (for update, to authenticated, using true / with check true; admin-gated at the app layer). LESSON: an RLS table the dashboard WRITES to needs a matching write policy; a missing one fails silently (0 rows, no error). **NEXT (top after-hours TODO):** add a dashboard link to leads.html (touches index.html).

### A from-scratch redesign stylesheet CANNOT be layered onto the legacy dashboard DOM (Session 122, 2026-06-21)
`design/dashboard.draft.css` uses generic selectors (`body`, `h1`, `.card`, `.badge`, `.stat`, a global `*` reset) written for the NEW prototype markup. Linking it AFTER `css/dashboard.css` on a copy of production (the `index.draft.html` experiment) made the page unreadable/unusable — the generic rules clobber the live DOM, which has a different structure/class set. The redesign is being pursued as a STANDALONE page (`design/board-live.html`) that fetches live data via the anon key, NOT by layering. Port to index.html only at the very end, as a deliberate full markup+CSS swap. RELATED GOTCHA: RLS policy `Anon can read repair_orders` = `using true`, so a browser CAN SELECT repair_orders with just the public anon key — no auth needed for read-only views (writes still require authenticated). Useful for standalone read-only previews/tools.

### To RE-SEND an ER completion email, reset completion_emailed_at AND re-flip status into done (Session 120, 2026-06-21)
`trg_notify_er_completion` only fires when `NEW.status='done' AND OLD.status IS DISTINCT FROM 'done' AND completion_emailed_at IS NULL`. So a plain UPDATE of completion_notes on an already-done ER does NOT re-email. To send a corrected/follow-up completion email: (1) `UPDATE ... SET status='in-progress', completion_emailed_at=null, completion_notes=...` then (2) `UPDATE ... SET status='done'`. The two-step makes OLD.status distinct from done with a null stamp, so the trigger re-fires and the edge fn reads the fresh completion_notes/test_steps at send time. Used S120 to re-send Lynn's 1aeb3f58 note (it sends a SECOND email, which is expected).

### "Off Lot - Returning" RO status is hardcoded in ~7 places — keep them in sync (Session 120, 2026-06-21)
The S120 status add (ER dac9fdda) had to touch every hardcoded status list: the index.html form `<select name="status">`, the status filter buttons, BOTH render.js card status dropdowns (compact ~L239 + standard ~L407), STATUS_PROGRESS_MAP (config.js + the inline copy in index.html ~L1204), and the ES translation map (config.js + inline ~L4038). It is also EXCLUDED from the on-lot count (render.js onLotCount, physically away) and given a statusColorMap accent (#0ea5e9). NOTE: its CSS slug `off-lot---returning` has no `.status-dropdown.status-*` rule, so the dropdown uses default tint (cosmetic only). Any future status add must hit all of these; grep `Waiting for QA/QC` to find every list.

### scheduled_notifications.source CHECK now allows `service_added_notify` (Session 120, 2026-06-21)
Migration `service_added_notify_source.sql` widened the CHECK to `manual, auto_dropoff_reminder, auto_promised_reminder, auto_pickup_reminder, service_added_notify`. The new source is used by work-orders.js addServiceToRO (ER 9b823d25) to queue a heads-up email to the newly-added silo's manager(s), sent by the every-15-min process-scheduled-notifications cron. The migration MUST be run before the feature works — without it the insert fails the CHECK and the non-fatal catch swallows it (no email, no error).

### work-list.js silo tag uses curly quotes (pre-existing, NOT introduced S120)
`js/work-list.js` ~line 298 builds the siloTag with curly double-quotes inside the inline `style=` attribute instead of straight quotes, which breaks that tag's styling. Spotted during the fd6c122d touch-drag work and left untouched for scope. Logged as a 🔵 TODO.

### `scheduled_notifications.source` has a CHECK constraint — widen it before adding a new source (Session 119, 2026-06-20)
Adding a new auto-reminder source SILENTLY fails the insert if the value is not in the CHECK. S119's Key Dates P3 reminders threw `violates check constraint "scheduled_notifications_source_check"` because the constraint was `('manual','auto_dropoff_reminder')` only — and the insert was wrapped in a DEBUG-gated try/catch, so it failed invisibly (promised_date saved but no reminder rows). Migration `key_dates_reminder_sources.sql` widened it to add `auto_promised_reminder` + `auto_pickup_reminder`. Lesson (same family as the parts_status CHECK): probe `pg_get_constraintdef` before inserting enum-like values, and remember `warn()` is DEBUG-gated so swallowed errors don't print.

### The ER completion-email trigger is LIVE in prod — marking an ER 'done' emails the requester (Session 119, 2026-06-20)
`trg_notify_er_completion` (AFTER UPDATE on enhancement_requests) fires `send-er-completion` (pg_net + vault `service_role_key`) on the transition INTO status='done', once (guarded by `completion_emailed_at`). So flipping an ER to Done now emails `submitted_by` what-was-done (`completion_notes`) + how-to-test (`test_steps`). Author those two textareas on the ER admin card BEFORE marking Done (updateERStatus captures them atomically; or use Save details first). If notes are blank it still sends a generic "your request is live" notice. To re-send, the row must transition done->other->done (or clear completion_emailed_at + re-fire the fn). DB-trigger->edge-fn via `net.http_post` + `vault.decrypted_secrets where name='service_role_key'` is the reusable pattern (mirrors the cron jobs; fires post-commit).

### Manager Daily Report admin COMBINED copy gets clipped by Gmail (Session 119, 2026-06-20)
The admin preview/copy renders all 9 manager cards in one email and exceeds Gmail's ~102KB clip threshold — Gmail shows "[Message clipped] … View entire message", so cards below ~Mauricio are hidden unless you expand. This is ONLY the admin combined copy; each manager's own daily send contains a single card and is not clipped. If it becomes annoying, trim the admin copy (e.g. summary-table + shop box only, or collapse cards). The new "Your Scheduled Reminders" section is forward-looking (today -> end of next week); overdue promised dates stay in Fire Watch by design.

### Check-in "duplicate ROs + RAFs not sending" = suspect a STALE CACHED kiosk page FIRST (Session 118, 2026-06-20)
When staff report both symptoms together, check the version badge at the bottom of the check-in page ON THE DEVICE before touching code. A cached **v1.10** produces both: the pre-v1.11 `getSignatureDataURL` typo aborted every RAF, and pre-v1.12 had no dup-RO guard. No service worker, so a long-open kiosk tab never re-fetches — the GitHub Pages server can be current while the device runs old JS. v1.13 hardened the dedupe to a submit-time phone/email lookup so duplicates can't happen even on a current page when staff skip the search. If RAFs still fail after the device shows v1.13, it's the inbox (RAF goes to the customer email + info@ CC, not repair@).

### Keys/Power fields are free text — key_status has NO CHECK constraint (Session 118, 2026-06-20)
`repair_orders.key_status` (keys / no_keys / keypad), `keypad_code`, `keep_plugged_in` added v1.458 (migration `keys_power_fields.sql`). key_status is intentionally free text (no CHECK) so new values never need a migration — the app constrains the options. Cards show a keys/power chip row (render.js). NOTE: keys were added to the DASHBOARD New/Edit RO only, NOT customer-checkin.html yet (ER 34fc03c2 closed on the dashboard piece; the check-in capture is a future extension if wanted).

### Worklist auto-prune is live — cashed-out ROs drop off manager worklists the day after (Session 118, 2026-06-20)
`prune_cashiered_worklists()` + daily cron `prune-cashiered-worklists [30 7 * * *]` (migration `prune_cashiered_worklists.sql`). Removes manager_work_lists rows where the RO is 'Delivered/Cashed Out' AND `(updated_at AT TIME ZONE 'America/Chicago')::date < today` — so it stays the day it's cashed out, drops the next day. ro_id is TEXT holding the uuid -> `::uuid` cast required. Editing a long-ago cashed-out RO today resets updated_at and keeps it one extra day (harmless).

### Key Dates Phase 1 live (v1.457) + fixed Edit-RO nulling planned_dropoff_date (Session 117, 2026-06-18)
NEW `repair_orders.pickup_date` (additive date, migration `key_dates_pickup_date.sql`). Pickup/Completed input added to New RO + Edit RO; the Edit RO form also REGAINED a Planned Drop Off input. BEFORE v1.457 the Edit RO form had NO drop-off input, so the edit form-data builder (index.html ~5847) never gathered it and **every Edit-RO save wrote `planned_dropoff_date = null`** (wiping its morning-before reminder). Now both fields are on the edit form, gathered in the builder, and populated in `openEditRO` (ro-crud.js). RO cards show a colored key-date chip row (blue Drop / amber Promised — red if past-due and still open / green Pickup) via an IIFE in render.js. `normalizeRO` has TWO copies (js/utils.js + the index.html inline copy ~4650) — keep `pickupDate` in sync across both. **Phase 2 gotcha:** writing Google Calendar events for the promised/pickup dates needs an interactive Google access token (manager signed in) — same constraint as the 📅 Schedule modal; resolve the token approach before building. Full plan: `docs/specs/KEY_DATES_SPEC.md`.

### scrub_soft_deleted_ros() was silently failing for 8+ days — check cron.job_run_details (Session 115, 2026-06-17)
The nightly auto-purge (cron jobid 6 `scrub-soft-deleted-ros`, `0 7 * * *`) had failed EVERY run for 8+ days with `operator does not exist: text = uuid` (the `manager_work_lists` delete), so soft-deleted ROs never purged and the Recently Deleted bucket filled with "overdue" rows. The cron job + function existed and were `active=true` — the failure was only visible in `cron.job_run_details` (status='failed', return_message). LESSON: an active cron job is NOT proof it succeeds — check `SELECT status, return_message FROM cron.job_run_details WHERE jobid=N ORDER BY start_time DESC`. Fixed in `fix_scrub_soft_deleted_ros.sql`: (1) `manager_work_lists.ro_id = target.id::text` (ro_id is TEXT holding the uuid — same gotcha as the manager report ::uuid cast); (2) replaced a `service_tasks.wo_id` (non-existent column) work-order loop with a direct `DELETE FROM service_tasks WHERE ro_id = target.id`. Defect 2 was masked behind defect 1 until the first was fixed. **A "no cron job has failed its recent runs" DB invariant (audit_codebase.py Class J) would have caught this — candidate next invariant.**

### Hard-delete confirm matches internal whitespace exactly (Session 115, 2026-06-17)
`hardDeleteROnow` (index.html:~1610) confirms a permanent delete by `typed.trim() !== customerName.trim()` — it trims the ENDS but compares internal whitespace exactly. Several legacy test ROs have customer_names with DOUBLE spaces (e.g. "Bob Vernier  DELETE"), so a normal single-space typed name is rejected with "Name did not match." Workaround: type the exact stored spacing. Fix (🔵 TODO logged): normalize runs of whitespace before comparing — `s => s.trim().replace(/\s+/g,' ')` on both sides.

### `updated_at` is now trigger-maintained on all 14 tables — do NOT hand-set it (Session 115, 2026-06-17)
Migration `auto_set_updated_at.sql` adds a shared `public.set_updated_at()` function + a `trg_set_updated_at` BEFORE UPDATE trigger on every public table with an `updated_at` column (repair_orders, parts, service_work_orders, service_tasks, time_logs, time_off_requests, enhancement_requests, scheduled_notifications, app_config, config, users, solar_project_store, solar_settings, wo_task_templates). The trigger forces `updated_at = now()` on every UPDATE, so app code no longer needs to set it — any payload that still does is REDUNDANT (harmless; same value). Root cause it fixed: `updated_at` had NO trigger anywhere and app code set it inconsistently, so the S114 returning-customer dup-RO UPDATE branch left repair_orders.updated_at frozen at creation time. Nothing reads `updated_at` for logic today, so it was a silent gap (no symptom). `scripts/audit_codebase.py` Class I flags the 6 surviving manual writes (cleanup TODO logged 🔵). **Verify trigger coverage via `pg_trigger`, NOT `information_schema.triggers`** — the latter is privilege-filtered and returns [] under the read-only MCP even when the triggers exist (see Class J invariant SQL + the new memory note).

### audit_codebase.py gained Class I + Class J (Session 115, 2026-06-17)
Class I (static, JS_SCANNERS): flags `.update`/`.upsert` payloads that manually set `updated_at` on a trigger-covered table (redundant). Class J (NOT static — the script can't reach the DB): `render_db_invariants()` PRINTS catalog-invariant SQL into the report under "DB Invariants (run manually)", to be run via the read-only MCP / SQL editor. First invariant = "every table with an updated_at column has a maintaining trigger" (self-discovers from the catalog, returns 0 rows when healthy). This is the check-class that would have caught the updated_at gap on day one; feeds the future Fable deep-scan. To add more invariants, append `DbInvariant(...)` entries.

### Manager Daily Report P4 is LIVE — per-manager send is secret-gated; cron fires send mode (Session 111, 2026-06-16)
`send-manager-report` v2.1-P4 has TWO paths. **Admin-preview** (default; body `{}` or no `send`): one combined email to `app_config.admin_report_recipients` (Roland+Lynn) — still OPEN (anon Bearer is enough), acceptable because it only emails admins. **Per-manager send** (body `{"send":true}`): emails EACH active manager their own card; GATED behind the `x-prvs-secret` header (`PRVS_FUNCTION_SECRET`; same shared secret as send-quote-email, value in js/config.js `b8b5561b...`). Send mode FAILS SAFE — refuses (401) if the secret is unset or mismatched. In send mode the fn ALSO emails admins ONE combined "admin copy" (all cards + the shop-spend box) — there is NO per-email admin CC (Roland dropped the spec D4 CC for a cleaner inbox). **Cron jobid 5 now fires send mode** (`cron.alter_job` set body `{"send":true}` + the secret header; schedule unchanged `0 12 * * 1-5` = 7AM CDT weekdays). To fire manually: `curl -X POST .../functions/v1/send-manager-report -H "Authorization: Bearer <anon>" -H "x-prvs-secret: <PRVS_FUNCTION_SECRET>" -d '{"send":true}'`. To get an admin-only preview without emailing managers: same curl with `-d '{}'` and no secret. Shop ROs are matched by `customer_name ILIKE '%shop operations%'` (two of them) and their parts are excluded from the parts-manager silo-less list + surfaced only in the admin shop-spend box. Edge fn is on pre-prod `790e925` only (not promoted to main).

### Gmail collapses repeated identical blocks in a multi-record email ("•••" trimmed content) (Session 110, 2026-06-14)
The Manager Daily Report admin preview renders all ~10 managers in ONE email. v1 repeated the same multi-sentence "why/how" footer under every manager card; Gmail's dedup heuristic collapsed the repeats behind `•••` "show trimmed content" toggles, making the digest unreadable (also bloats toward Gmail's ~102 KB clip limit). FIX: put shared explanatory prose in ONE legend at the top, keep per-card content unique (data + short contextual `↳` breadcrumbs). Rule: in any digest-style email that loops over records, never repeat large verbatim text blocks per record. Note this is a digest-only problem — the P4 per-manager emails (one manager each) won't hit it.

### Manager Daily Report P1 is LIVE + admin-preview only (Session 110, 2026-06-14)
`send-manager-report` is now v2.0-P1: it sends ONE combined all-managers email to ADMINS ONLY (`app_config.admin_report_recipients` = Roland+Lynn). No individual manager receives mail until P4. Cron jobid 5 fires 7 AM CDT weekdays (`0 12 * * 1-5`). The edge fn has NO X-PRVS-Secret / JWT check of its own (it just runs); the cron authorizes via a Bearer header already baked into the job command. Anyone with the anon key can fire it (test: `curl -X POST .../functions/v1/send-manager-report -H "Authorization: Bearer <anon>" -d '{}'`) — acceptable for P1 since it only ever emails admins, but ADD a secret check before P4 flips on real manager sends. Implemented readiness checks = R1/R2/R3/R5/R7/R8/R9 (R4 unattributed-labor + R6 phantom-hours deferred to P2+). DONE/excluded-from-fires status set = 'Delivered/Cashed Out' + 'Ready for pickup'. Idle = no tech time in 5 WORK days (business-day calc).

### Manager report build — data gotchas + guards (Session 109, 2026-06-14)
For the Manager Daily Report build (top TODO), three things learned validating the rule engine on live data: **(1)** `manager_work_lists.ro_id` is **TEXT holding the RO UUID** — joins to `repair_orders.id` (uuid) need an explicit cast: `JOIN repair_orders r ON r.id = m.ro_id::uuid` (raw join throws `operator does not exist: uuid = text`). **(2)** Sentinel/invalid dates exist — at least one RO has `promised_date = 0001-01-01`, which naively reads as ~739,780 days overdue. Guard: a promised/ETA date only counts as a real Fire Watch flag when sane (year >= 2020); invalid dates become their own "fix this date" readiness flag, not an overdue fire. **(3)** Junk/soft-deleted `…DELETE` and training ROs appear on lists — apply the standard exclusion filter (soft-deleted + `is_training`) BEFORE computing flags/readiness, or they pollute both the fires and the readiness denominator. Full validated baseline (Ryan, 21 ROs, 48% readiness) is in `docs/specs/MANAGER_DAILY_REPORT_SPEC.md` sec 10.5.

### guide.html anchor ids are a CONTRACT — don't rename without updating the linkers (Session 113, 2026-06-16)
Five places now deep-link into `guide.html` by anchor: index.html (header Guide button is anchorless, but the WO build form links `#build-wo`), js/work-orders.js (`#build-wo`), js/parts.js (`#part-silo`), checkin.html (`#tech`), `send-manager-report` (per-block `guideLink()` -> `#rb-active #rb-idle #rb-firewatch #rb-readiness #rb-parts`), `send-parts-report` (`#parts-managers`). The full live anchor set: `#report-glossary #start-here #report-walkthrough #rb-active #rb-idle #rb-firewatch #rb-readiness #rb-parts #rb-phantom #tech #tech-step-1..5 #phantom-hours #silo-managers #build-wo #mark-completed #part-silo #part-cost #parts-managers #flags #whats-next`. Renaming any of these silently breaks an in-app or email link (no error, just lands at page top). Verify with the python "every guide.html#anchor resolves" check (run S113) after any guide edit. Note the report emails link to the PRODUCTION url, so guide.html must be on `main` before the edge fns are deployed (the reason S113 was a full prod rollout, not a soak). **S116 added a top "full instructions" banner to all 3 report emails:** `send-parts-report` -> `#parts-managers`, `send-manager-report` (admin + per-manager bodies) + `send-admin-pnl-report` -> `#report-glossary`. Both anchors are already live on guide.html (on main since S113), so these were safe to deploy without re-shipping guide.html — but if `#report-glossary` or `#parts-managers` is ever renamed, all three report banners break too.

### service_work_orders.estimated_hours is a BASIC-WO fallback only (Session 109, 2026-06-14)
`service_tasks` already has `est_hours` / `actual_hours` / `billed_hours` per sub-item, and the WO build form + card already capture/show task-level estimates (68% of active WOs have them). The new WO-level `service_work_orders.estimated_hours` (v1.451) is a FALLBACK for "basic" task-less WOs only. The effective WO estimate everywhere = **sum of task `est_hours` when the WO has tasks, else the WO-level `estimated_hours`** (COALESCE — tasks win, never double-count). The WO modal field is always shown but its helper text says it is ignored once tasks exist. Don't add a second always-on WO-level entry path or you create two sources of truth.

### Sendblue: from_number now REQUIRED, is_imessage only via webhook, + secrets moved (Session 108, 2026-06-14)
FOUR Sendblue gotchas from the Phase 2 rollout: **(1)** Sendblue's `/api/send-message` now REQUIRES a `from_number` param (which line sends) — without it you get HTTP 502 + `missing required parameter: "from_number"`. `sendblue-send` was patched to send it: default shared sandbox line `+16466208124`, overridable via the `SENDBLUE_FROM_NUMBER` secret (set it to the hosted office number 940-488-5047 at production cutover). **(2)** `is_imessage` (Sendblue `was_downgraded`) is NOT in the send-message response — it is null at queue time for BOTH iMessage and SMS sends and only resolves once the message delivers, via the delivery-status WEBHOOK (deferred, Q7). The flag stays null until `sendblue-webhook` is built. **(3)** Supabase moved edge-function secrets OUT of Project Settings — they now live under **Edge Functions → Secrets** (`/dashboard/project/<ref>/functions/secrets`), NOT Settings → Edge Functions (which no longer exists in the Settings sidebar). **(4)** The free shared line (`+1 646 620 8124`, 10-contact cap) reaches VERIFIED contacts only — add a contact in the Sendblue console first or outbound errors/drops. POC tested on localhost:8765 (the origin sendblue-send CORS allows); the POC branch is v1.448 (cut pre-v1.449/v1.450 — that version "mismatch" vs prod is expected, not a bug).

### CLAUDE_CONTEXT_ARCHIVE.md is COLD — do not read it at session start (Session 107, 2026-06-14)
Session 107 split the context docs into three tiers: `CLAUDE_CONTEXT.md` (hot, read every session), `CLAUDE_CONTEXT_HISTORY.md` (warm, recent-only — Session ≥97 / dated ≥2026-06-01), and NEW `CLAUDE_CONTEXT_ARCHIVE.md` (cold, ~660 KB). Start/Pause/End Session read ONLY the first two. The ARCHIVE holds old Session Log prose, completed TODOs, the File Inventory back-catalog, resolved/removed-system Known Issues, and HISTORY for Sessions ≤96 — open it ONLY for deep historical analysis. Nothing was deleted; everything was relocated (zero-loss verified). Backups live in `.context_backups/` (gitignored). Roland may later want HISTORY/ARCHIVE made fully on-demand — revisit then.

### audit_log has two FK traps — user_id FK→users(id) and ro_id ON DELETE CASCADE (Session 105, 2026-06-13)
`audit_log.user_id` is a FK to `users(id)`. Inserting an audit row with a `user_id` that is NOT a `public.users` row (e.g. a tech clocking in at the kiosk — most techs have no users row) raises an FK violation. If the insert is in a non-fatal try/catch (as the checkin auto-flip was), the audit row silently vanishes. **Rule: for any kiosk/automated audit write, pass `user_id: null`** and keep attribution in `user_email` + `user_name` (this is how the S103 WO-flip trigger and the v1.36 clock-in fix both do it). Diagnostic that exposed it: only 6 `'auto via clock-in'` audit rows existed vs 25 `AUTO-STATUS` notes from the same code block — the 6 were Roland/Jason, who ARE in users. SECOND trap: `audit_log.ro_id` is FK→`repair_orders(id)` **ON DELETE CASCADE** — when an RO is cashiered/deleted its audit history cascade-deletes too (mirrors the cashiered_time_logs problem). Ghost-write detection query: compare current `repair_orders.status` to the last `field_changed='status'` audit_log.new_value; mismatch + `updated_at` later = an unaudited status write.

### Clock-in RO auto-flip is allowlist-guarded as of v1.36 — do not widen it casually (Session 105, 2026-06-13)
`checkin.html` clockIn only advances status from `FLIPPABLE_STATUSES = ['', 'Not On Lot', 'On Lot', 'Scheduled', 'Ready to Work']`. It deliberately does NOT flip Awaiting parts / Awaiting Approval (manager decision states) or any completed-side status (Repairs Completed / Waiting for QA/QC / Ready for pickup / Delivered) — Roland's explicit S105 decision after a scenario walk-through (preserve both Awaiting states; a clock-in on a completed RO leaves it put). A clock-in is still recorded in time_logs + the AUTO-STATUS note even when the status is preserved, so no information is lost. If a future request asks to "auto-advance on clock-in," confirm whether it should override these preserved states before changing the allowlist.

### Training docs are GENERATED — edit scripts/docgen, do not hand-edit the docx (Session 104, 2026-06-12)
`docs/PRVS_Tech_and_Lead_RO_Check_In_Procedure.*` and `docs/PRVS_PnL_Manager_Guide.*` are built by `scripts/docgen/make_quickcard.js` and `make_manager_guide.js` (node, `npm install docx`, then soffice headless for the pdf). To change wording: edit the EN/ES string objects in the script, regenerate both docx+pdf, keep EN and ES in sync (Roland's S104 PDF markup only changed EN — the ES page had to be re-mirrored manually). Emoji like 🟢🔴✅ render as tofu boxes in the LibreOffice pdf export — use colored bold text instead. Each language page must stay exactly 1 page (tech card); check `pdfinfo` page count after any edit.

### Kiosk clock-in is SINGLE-service by design + time_logs now carries TWO triggers (Session 103, 2026-06-12)
A tech cannot clock into more than one service at once (Roland, S103) — do not design features assuming comma-multi service_type from checkin.html; the comma-split handling in the weekly_pnl RPC and the new trigger is legacy/defensive coverage only. time_logs triggers: `trg_auto_close_prior_open_session` (BEFORE INSERT, GH#33) + `trg_auto_flip_wo_in_progress` (AFTER INSERT, S103 — flips matching silo WO not_started→in_progress, upgrade-only, audit-logged `wo_status:<silo>`). Any future time_logs INSERT path (offline replay, backfills, scripts) WILL fire both.

### weekly_pnl targets DO work — admin report lacks targets BY DESIGN until v2 (Session 103)
The S101 “NULL targets” sighting was not reproducible: RPC + seeds + grants verified, live page renders targets for weeks ≥ effective_date 2026-06-08. send-admin-pnl-report v1 deliberately has no target wiring — that is v2 roadmap item (a), not a bug.

### Any historical time_logs feature MUST union the cashiered_time_logs mirror (Session 102, 2026-06-11)
The Saturday archiver hard-deletes a cashiered RO's `time_logs` rows from the live table (snapshotting them into `cashiered_time_logs` as JSONB envelopes: `source_data` = full original row, `original_ro_id`, FK `cashiered_id -> cashiered(id)` CASCADE). So ANY feature reading historical labor from live `time_logs` alone silently loses every since-archived RO — past weeks look mysteriously quiet (the Session 102 calendar v1.17 bug; the weekly_pnl RPCs already union the mirrors, which is why the P&L was right while the calendar was wrong). Patterns that work: PostgREST embed `cashiered:cashiered_id(ro_id, customer_name, rv)` for labels; range-filter via `.gte('source_data->>clock_in', iso)` with the ISO suffix rewritten `'Z' -> '+00:00'` to match to_jsonb's timestamp rendering (string comparison). No double-count risk: archiving deletes live rows, reactivation CASCADE-deletes mirrors. NOTE: `cashiered` has NO `is_training` column — tester-email exclusion is the only filter available for archived rows.

### weekly_pnl RPC silo-attribution ORDER: Shop check comes FIRST, before the pin (Session 102)
The RPC's CASE order is: service_type 'shop' -> overhead REGARDLESS of `staff.pnl_home_silo`; THEN pin; THEN service_type map; THEN overhead. Client-side re-implementations must match the ORDER, not just the rules — the calendar v1.17 checked the pin first and pinned techs' Shop time inflated their silo's hours vs the P&L matrix. Canonical client copy: `pcalSiloForLog()` in worklist-report.html.

### worklist-report version pill = single WLR_VERSION constant (Session 102)
worklist-report.html now has a visible version pill (header-right) driven by `const WLR_VERSION` at the top of the main script block. Every release bumps exactly TWO sites: the header comment (line 3) + WLR_VERSION. Do NOT hardcode the version anywhere else (the checkin.html third-bump-site lesson from Session 100).

### GitHub Pages CDN: hard refresh may NOT be enough — use a cache-bust query param (Session 102)
At the v1.18 prod verify, cmd+shift+R hard reload still served stale v1.17 minutes after the push. `?cb=<anything>` on the URL busted it instantly (unique URL bypasses both CDN and browser cache). Cheaper and more reliable than waiting out the ~10-min max-age during regressions.

### manager_work_lists.ro_id holds the repair_orders UUID, NOT the RO code (Session 101, 2026-06-11)
Despite the column name, `manager_work_lists.ro_id` (text) stores `repair_orders.id` (uuid). Join on `repair_orders.id`, then display `repair_orders.ro_id` (the PRVS-XXXX code). Bit the admin report's first test fire (0 managers matched).

### Unattributed P&L silo is PARTS-ONLY by design (Session 101)
Labor can never land in Unattributed — the RPC chain is: service_type 'shop' -> overhead; else staff.pnl_home_silo pin; else parseable service_type; else **overhead** fallback. Unattributed = parts with `service_silo IS NULL` on ROs with any silo activity that week. The drill-down's per-RO hours/labor there are the RO's FULL-week labor shown for context (already attributed to real silos in the rows above) — only the parts dollars are actually unattributed.

### Claude-in-Chrome "Grouping is not supported by tabs in this window" — use Control_Chrome AppleScript MCP as fallback (Session 101)
`tabs_context_mcp` failed repeatedly even on a normal window. Fallback that WORKS: the Control_Chrome (AppleScript) MCP — `open_url`, `list_tabs`, `execute_javascript`. CAVEAT: its JS runs in an ISOLATED WORLD — page globals/functions are invisible (`typeof pnlToggleSilo` = undefined, `supabaseSession` = undefined) but the DOM is shared. Drive the page via DOM clicks (`element.click()` fires inline onclick handlers in the page context) and assert on DOM state, not JS globals.

### Admin report cron is UTC — 6 AM CDT becomes 5 AM CST when DST ends (Session 101)
`send-admin-pnl-report-daily` = `0 11 * * 1-5`. Change to `0 12 * * 1-5` at the November DST flip (same applies to the 7 AM ER digest pattern).

### GitHub Release URL-prefill trick — bypasses the extension-popup publish fight (Session 100, 2026-06-10)
`github.com/<org>/<repo>/releases/new?tag=v1.XXX&target=main&title=<urlencoded>&body=<urlencoded>` prefills the ENTIRE release form (tag picker resolves to "Existing tag", title + markdown body populated). Only the Publish click remains — a plain coordinate-click on the green button worked first try. This beats the recurring Sessions 93/95 quirk chain (chrome-extension:// popup killing click/screenshot, ref-clicks never submitting the form). Build the URL with python urllib.parse.urlencode. Use this for every future release.

### RAF email pipeline verified HEALTHY (Session 114) — future "RAF not sent" reports are inbox/trigger, not backend
S114 live test-fired the deployed `send-quote-email` `raf_copy` (to roland@) and got HTTP 200 `{success:true}` — the edge fn, its secrets (GMAIL_USER / GMAIL_APP_PASSWORD / PRVS_FUNCTION_SECRET), the Gmail send, and the signature attachment all work. `sendRAFEmail` (customer-checkin.html ~L2346) and the `raf_copy` branch are intact (getSignatureData + `node:buffer` import both present). So if anyone reports "the RAF wasn't emailed," check these BEFORE touching code: (1) RAF copy goes to the CUSTOMER email with info@ CC'd — NOT repair@; if no customer email was entered it goes to info@ only; (2) RAF only fires on a signed DROP-OFF (`formState.mode === 'dropoff'`), not New Customer Entry / lead. To verify the deployed fn anytime, POST raf_copy with the anon Bearer + X-PRVS-Secret (both in config.js) from an authenticated page console.

### ER admin status dropdown is HARDCODED (Session 114)
`render.js` `renderERAdminList` (~L730) hardcodes the status `<select>` options to `['unreviewed','reviewed','planned','in-progress','done','declined']` and a matching `statusColors` map (~L717). Writing an off-list status (e.g. a literal "in prod testing") makes the chip render gray AND the dropdown shows the WRONG option selected (no matching `<option>`), risking an accidental flip on the next change. To add a new status you must edit BOTH the options array and statusColors (+ ship). S114 declined adding one and used `status='in-progress'` + an "IN PROD TESTING" admin_note instead.

### checkin.html visible version badge is a SEPARATE bump site (Session 100)
The `<div class="version">` near line 338 of checkin.html is not covered by the header-comment + boot-log version markers — it sat at v1.33 through both the v1.34 and v1.35 bumps until caught by the Session 100 PROD regression (page WAS serving v1.35; only the badge lied). Fixed on pre-prod `0c6da93`. Every checkin.html version bump must touch THREE sites: header comment, boot log line, AND the .version badge div.

### worklist-report.html logs a GSI "Missing required parameter: client_id" console error (observed Session 100)
Seen during the v1.449 PROD regression; the page fully loads + renders P&L data regardless. Almost certainly pre-existing Google sign-in plumbing noise (not introduced by the P&L changes — config.js delta was version-only). Low priority; investigate only if sign-in on that page misbehaves.

### parts.core_charge stores FREIGHT, not a core charge (Session 99, 2026-06-10)
The Add/Edit Part form labels the `core_charge` column "Freight Charge ($)". Roland-confirmed semantics: `wholesale_price` is PER UNIT, freight is PER LINE → part cost = `wholesale * qty + core_charge`. The weekly_pnl RPCs use this basis; any future parts math MUST too. (Also largely satisfies ER n28's freight ask — the data was there all along.)

### Weekly P&L attribution + access rules (Session 99)
`staff.pnl_home_silo` pin ALWAYS beats the clock-in service_type ("if Rod/Zak/Travis log time, the RV is in their bay" — Roland); 'Shop' clock-ins → overhead regardless; floaters (Cooper/Tommy/Riley/managers) attribute by clock-in pick. Techs CANNOT write service_work_orders under RLS — the checkin tech-Done button uses the `mark_wo_tech_done` SECURITY DEFINER RPC (sets ONLY tech_done_at/by). Manager "✓ Mark Completed" = revenue recognition; Reopen moves it back out. weekly_pnl/weekly_pnl_detail gates: SQL-editor/service-role pass (auth.uid() NULL), authenticated non-admins rejected, anon can't EXECUTE — the read-only Supabase MCP also cannot execute them (validate via SQL editor).

### v1.450 lives on branch `chore/parts-status-cleanup` — NOT yet on pre-prod/main (Session 106, 2026-06-14)
Removes the dead parts_status='outstanding' render alias (4 js/render.js + 3 js/parts.js fallbacks).
